            <pd:activity name="UpdateToODS">
                <pd:type>com.tibco.plugin.jdbc.JDBCUpdateActivity</pd:type>
                <pd:resourceType>ae.activities.JDBCUpdateActivity</pd:resourceType>
                <pd:x>485</pd:x>
                <pd:y>400</pd:y>
                <config>
                    <timeout>%%Tuning/Connections/Database/JDBCQuery/QueryTimeout%%</timeout>
                    <commit>false</commit>
                    <emptyStrAsNil>false</emptyStrAsNil>
                    <jdbcSharedConfig>/SharedResources/Connections/Database/CC2ODSJDBCConnection.sharedjdbc</jdbcSharedConfig>
                    <statement>UPDATE CC_ODS_ACCOUNT_ADDITIONAL_ATTR
SET  BILLING_CYCLE=?,
DELINQUENCY_MONTHS =?
WHERE
(
ACCOUNT_NBR=? AND
ACCOUNT_TYPE_CD=? AND
RETAIL_DIV_NBR=? AND
CARD_HOLDER_TYPE_ID=?
)</statement>
                    <Prepared_Param_DataType>
                        <parameter>
                            <parameterName>BILL_CYCLE</parameterName>
                            <dataType>INTEGER</dataType>
                        </parameter>
                        <parameter>
                            <parameterName>DELINQUENCY_MONTHS</parameterName>
                            <dataType>INTEGER</dataType>
                        </parameter>
                        <parameter>
                            <parameterName>ACCOUNT_NBR</parameterName>
                            <dataType>BIGINT</dataType>
                        </parameter>
                        <parameter>

                        </parameter>

                            <parameterName>CARD_HOLDER_TYPE_ID</parameterName>
                            <dataType>VARCHAR</dataType>
                        </parameter>
                    </Prepared_Param_DataType>
                </config>
                <pd:inputBindings>
                    <jdbcUpdateActivityInput>
                        <BILL_CYCLE>
                            <xsl:choose>
                                <xsl:when test="exists($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:BILL-CYCLE)">

                                <xsl:otherwise>
                                    <xsl:attribute name="xsi:nil">true</xsl:attribute>
                                </xsl:otherwise>
                            </xsl:choose>
                        </BILL_CYCLE>
                        <DELINQUENCY_MONTHS>
                            <xsl:choose>
                                <xsl:when test="exists($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CHD-DEL-NMO-CONT)">
                                    <xsl:value-of select="$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CHD-DEL-NMO-CONT"/>
                                </xsl:when>
                                <xsl:otherwise>
                                    <xsl:attribute name="xsi:nil">true</xsl:attribute>
                                </xsl:otherwise>
                            </xsl:choose>
                        </DELINQUENCY_MONTHS>
                        <ACCOUNT_NBR>
                            <xsl:choose>
                                <xsl:when test="exists(if (string-length($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR)>0 &#xA;and $CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR>0 &#xA;and $CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR !=$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER)&#xA;then&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR&#xA;else if (string-length($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR)>0 and&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR>0 and&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR !=$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-AMEX-NBR&#xA;)&#xA;then&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR&#xA;else if (string-length($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER)>0 and&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER>0&#xA;)&#xA;then&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER&#xA;else&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-AMEX-NBR)">
                                    <xsl:value-of select="if (string-length($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR)>0 &#xA;and $CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR>0 &#xA;and $CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR !=$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER)&#xA;then&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-PL-NBR&#xA;else if (string-length($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR)>0 and&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR>0 and&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR !=$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-AMEX-NBR&#xA;)&#xA;then&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:NEW-AMEX-NBR&#xA;else if (string-length($CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER)>0 and&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER>0&#xA;)&#xA;then&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-PL-NUMBER&#xA;else&#xA;$CurrCreditRecord/pfx6:CreditRecord/pfx6:CURRENT-AMEX-NBR"/>

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<xs:schema xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema"
	 xmlns="http://www.tibco.com/schemas/BAFBWClient/SharedResources/Schemas/BAFBWClient/CommonSchema.xsd"
	 targetNamespace="http://www.tibco.com/schemas/BAFBWClient/SharedResources/Schemas/BAFBWClient/CommonSchema.xsd"
	 elementFormDefault="qualified"
	 attributeFormDefault="unqualified">
	<xs:element name="Name" type="xs:string"/>
	<xs:element name="Value" type="xs:string"/>
	<xs:element name="BusinessProperties">
		<xs:complexType>
			<xs:sequence>
				<xs:element ref="Name"/>
				<xs:element ref="Value"/>
			</xs:sequence>
		</xs:complexType>
	</xs:element>
	<xs:element name="PlaceHolder" type="xs:string"/>
	<xs:element name="ValidFlag" type="xs:boolean"/>
	<xs:element name="EngineID" type="xs:string"/>
	<xs:element name="Action">
		<xs:simpleType>
			<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
				<xs:enumeration value="STOP"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="PAUSE"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="RESUME"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="START"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="GETSTATUS"/>
			</xs:restriction>
		</xs:simpleType>
	</xs:element>
	<xs:element name="Status">
		<xs:simpleType>
			<xs:restriction base="xs:string">
				<xs:enumeration value="PENDING"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="READY"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="STARTED"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="RUNNING"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="PAUSED"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="RESUME"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="ERROR"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="COMPLETED"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="SKIPPED"/>
				<xs:enumeration value="VALIDATING"/>
			</xs:restriction>
		</xs:simpleType>
	</xs:element>
	<xs:element name="JobID" type="xs:string"/>

	<xs:element name="StartDateTime" type="xs:dateTime"/>
	<xs:element name="EndDateTime" type="xs:dateTime"/>

				<xs:element ref="JobQueuePosition" minOccurs="0"/>
				<xs:element ref="JobQueueGroup" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
				<xs:element ref="Exception" minOccurs="0"/>
				<xs:element ref="PendingAction" minOccurs="0"/>
				<xs:element ref="Notification" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
			</xs:sequence>
		</xs:complexType>
	</xs:element>
	<xs:element name="JobQueue">
		<xs:complexType>
			<xs:sequence>
				<xs:element ref="SequenceNumber" minOccurs="0"/>
				<xs:element ref="BusinessProperties" minOccurs="0" maxOccurs="unbounded"/>
			</xs:sequence>
		</xs:complexType>
	</xs:element>
	<xs:element name="TriggerDateTime" type="xs:dateTime"/>

	<xs:element name="BatchName" type="xs:string"/>

	<xs:element name="AssociationCount" type="xs:long"/>

			</xs:sequence>
		</xs:complexType>
	</xs:element>
